***матовый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:матовый.html>ма́товый</a> (7317)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>мат</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn"><a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>mat</a></span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">matte</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:матовый.html>ма́товый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mátovyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ма́товее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ма́товей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>matte, dull, lustreless
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:матовый.html>ма́товая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:поверхность.html>пове́рхность</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mátovaja</b> povérxnostʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>dead</b> surface, <b>matte</b> surface</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:матовый.html>ма́товое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:золото.html>зо́лото</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mátovoje</b> zóloto</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>matte</b> gold</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:матовый.html>ма́товая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кожа.html>ко́жа</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mátovaja</b> kóža</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>matte</b> leather</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>opaque, frosted
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:матовый.html>ма́товое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:стекло.html>стекло́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mátovoje</b> stekló</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>frosted</b> glass</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:матка.html>ма́тка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mátka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:маточный.html>ма́точный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mátočnyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> uterus, womb; uterine
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:маточный.html>ма́точная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:железо.html>железа́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mátočnaja</b> železá</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>uterine</b> gland</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:маточный.html>ма́точная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:труба.html>труба́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mátočnaja</b> trubá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Fallopian tube, <b>uterine</b> tube, salpinx</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> queen bee
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:маточный.html>ма́точное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:молочко.html>молочко́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mátočnoje</b> moločkó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">royal jelly</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Diminutive form of female name <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">Матрёна</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Matrjóna</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">mātrōna</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">matron</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***матросский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:матросский.html>матро́сский</a> (14235)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:матрос.html>матро́с</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">matrós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sailor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<h4><span id=".D0.A1.D0.B8.D0.BD.D0.BE.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.BC.D1.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Синонимы"><a href = vnd.unilang:синоним.html>Сино́нимы</a></span></h4>

***мах.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мах.html>мах</a> (7805)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>маха́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">maxátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мах.html>мах</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">max</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мах.html>ма́ха</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мах.html>ма́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мах.html>ма́хов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>single rapid movement in the air, swing, wave, flap, stroke</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rapid forward, backward or sideways movement of the foot or hand</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mechanics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> single revolution, swing, stroke</li>
<li>step <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of an animal, usually a horse, when running</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***махать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>маха́ть</a> (2480)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*māxàti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>маха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">maxátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махнуть.html>махну́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помахать.html>помаха́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wave, to flap, to fling, to brandish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">кто́-то <b><a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>ма́шет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руко́й</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Któ-to <b>mášet</b> tebé rukój.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Someone is <b>waving</b> a hand at you.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:махина.html>махи́на</a> (20034)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махина.html>махи́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">maxína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махина.html>махи́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махина.html>махи́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махина.html>махи́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> something big, a bulky and cumbersome thing</li></ol>

***махнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:махнуть.html>махну́ть</a> (1650)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махнуть.html>махну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">maxnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махать.html>маха́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wave, to flap, to fling, to brandish
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помнить.html>по́мнишь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:махнуть.html>махну́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руко́й</a>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pómnišʹ, kak ty <b>maxnúl</b> mne čérez dorógu rukój?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Do you remember how you <b>waved</b> at me across the road?</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:махнуть.html>махну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руко́й</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>maxnútʹ</b> rukój (na)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to give up on someone / something</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rush, to leap, to jump
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:махнуть.html>махну́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:через.html>че́рез</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:забор.html>забо́р</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>maxnúl</b> čérez zabór.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He <b>leapt</b> over the fence.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go (off), to travel
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:давать.html>дава́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:махнуть.html>махнём</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыбалка.html>рыба́лку</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Daváj <b>maxnjóm</b> na rybálku!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Let's go fishing!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to swap
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:махнуть.html>махну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глядеть.html>гля́дя</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>maxnútʹ</b> ne gljádja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">swap without looking (i.e. recklessly)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***махорка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:махорка.html>махо́рка</a> (10181)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Modification of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*амерфо́ртский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*amerfórtskij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Amersfoort" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Amersfoort">Amersfoort</a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from the Dutch city of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Amersfoort" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Amersfoort">Amersfoort</a>, known for its tobacco industries.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махорка.html>махо́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">maxórka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махорка.html>махо́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махорка.html>махо́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махорка.html>махо́рок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A coarse, strong type of tobacco, makhorka (<i>Nicotiana rustica</i>)</li></ol>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">7) <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> толстожилистыми пузырчатыми <a href = vnd.unilang:лист.html>ли́стьями</a> (Nicotiana angustifola var. andulata), <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a>, напр., амерсфортский <a href = vnd.unilang:табак.html>таба́к</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:разводимый.html>разводи́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> Голландии <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отличаться.html>отличающийся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́ю</a> урожайностью. <a href = vnd.unilang:последний.html>После́дний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сорт.html>сорт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:некоторый.html>не́которые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сельский.html>се́льские</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хозяин.html>хозя́ева</a> (напр., проф. Стебут) <a href = vnd.unilang:считать.html>счита́ют</a> однородным <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> возделываемой <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нас</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:махорка.html>махо́ркой</a></span> (<a href = vnd.unilang:объяснять.html>объясня́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:происхождение.html>происхожде́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>слова</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:название.html>назва́ния</a> амерфорка), <a href = vnd.unilang:который.html>кото́рая</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:табак.html>таба́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:убираться.html>убира́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отдельный.html>отде́льными</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лист.html>ли́стьями</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:целый.html>це́лыми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:растение.html>расте́ниями</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:часто.html>ча́сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:называться.html>называ́ется</a> амерсфортской рубанкой. <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>Но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уверение.html>увере́нию</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>други́х</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a>. <p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махра.html>махра́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">maxrá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махра.html>махры́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> makhorka <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a strong type of tobacco</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махра.html>махра́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">maxrá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махра.html>махры́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махровый.html>махро́вый</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махра.html>махра́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">maxrá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-óvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:махровый.html>махро́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">maxróvyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> terry cloth
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:махровый.html>махро́вое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:полотенце.html>полоте́нце</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>maxróvoje</b> poloténce</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>terry</b> towel</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> double
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:махровый.html>махро́вая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:роза.html>ро́за</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>maxróvaja</b> róza</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>double</b> rose</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> inveterate, double-dyed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:махровый.html>махро́вый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:негодяй.html>негодя́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>maxróvyj</b> negodjáj</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>double-dyed</b> rascal</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:махровый.html>махро́вый</a></b> реакционе́р</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>maxróvyj</b> reakcionér</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>inveterate</b> reactionary</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***мачта.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мачта.html>ма́чта</a> (7853)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From older <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ма́шта</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mášta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">mast</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">mast</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">maszt/maszta</i>. For the change <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-шт-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-št-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> → <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-чт-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-čt-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почта.html>по́чта</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">póčta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мачта.html>ма́чта</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">máčta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мачта.html>ма́чты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мачта.html>ма́чты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мачта.html>ма́чт</a></b>)
</p>

<li><i>(radio, electric)</i> tower</li></ol>

***машина.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́на</a> (167)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Maschine</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">machine, engine</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">machine</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">māchina</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">μαχανά</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">makhaná</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">machine, tool</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mašína</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> car, motor vehicle</li>
<li>machine</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> computer</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> accelerator</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mašína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машинка.html>маши́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mašínka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машинка.html>маши́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машинка.html>маши́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машинка.html>маши́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Diminutive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mašína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: small car, machine or mechanism</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">endearing form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mašína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li>
<li>miniature or toy car</li>
<li>small device for accomplishing work (e.g. typewriter, washing machine, clipper, etc.)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:швейный.html>шве́йная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:машинка.html>маши́нка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">švéjnaja mašínka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">sewing machine</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> typewriter</li></ol>
